id=\"overview-1d\">\n\t\t<p>Hide Price plugin enables the eCommerce functionality only for verified users. It provides a perfect platform for products which are accessible only for verified users. Admin just needs to set the password and give it to all the customers. Customers enter the password to access all eCommerce functionality including Buy Now, Add to Cart and Checkout process. Actually it hides the price and add to cart button from the product for non-verified users.</p><br>\n<h4>Features</h4><ul class=\"product-description-list\"><li>Hides product price and add to cart button.</li><li>Only verified users can get add to cart feature and can view the price.</li><li>Admin can enable or disable the effect of the extension.</li><li>Admin can give summary text for the product.</li><li>Admin can set password to hide the price and Add to Cart.</li><li>Admin can customize button text.</li><li>Admin can change the password field placeholder.</li><li>Admin can change the empty password message.</li><li>Admin can change the wrong password message.</li><li>Admin can change the matched password text/message.</li><li>Easy to use and customize.</li><li>WPML Compatible.</li><li>Translation Ready.</li></ul>\t</div>\n\t<h2 class=\"tab-mobile-heading\">\n\t\tUser Guide\n\t\t<span></span>\n\t\t<div class=\"clear\"></div>\n\t</h2>\n\t<div id=\"document\"
